                             == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                                                                                                                      
                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A Java OutOfMemoryError is triggered when processing a fuzzer-generated input in the Apache POI HMEF (TNEF) message handling code. The error arises during Unicode                  
                             string conversion in StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE, leading to heap exhaustion. The failure is reported by Jazzer as a low-severity security issue                                    
                             (FuzzerSecurityIssueLow).                                                                                                                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Issue Type                                                                                                                                                                        
                               The fuzzer run produced a `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space` in the Apache POI HMEF (Transport Neutral Encapsulation Format) processing code. Jazzer                   
                             classifies this as a low-severity security issue (`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`), specifically an out-of-memory condition that can be induced by crafted input.                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Observations & Findings                                                                                                                                                           
                               1. The exception stack trace shows the failure occurs in the constructor of `java.lang.String`, invoked from `org.apache.poi.util.StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`.                   
                               2. The code path begins in the TNEF message parser:                                                                                                                               
                                  - `org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.MAPIAttribute.create`                                                                                                                         
                                  - `org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.TNEFMAPIAttribute.<init>`                                                                                                                     
                                  - `org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.TNEFAttribute.create`                                                                                                                         
                                  - `org.apache.poi.hmef.HMEFMessage.processMessage`  `.process`  `<init>`                                                                                                     
                                  - Entry point `org.apache.poi.POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.                                                                                                               
                               3. The fuzzers command-line suggestion (`-Xmx921m`) indicates that limiting heap to 921 MB reproduces the out-of-memory error consistently.                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Vulnerability Classification                                                                                                                                                      
                               This is effectively a resource exhaustion vulnerability. An attacker supplying a specially crafted TNEF input can consume unbounded memory, resulting in a                        
                             denial-of-service condition.                                                                                                                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Code Areas for Investigation                                                                                                                                                      
                               To understand the full scope of the issue, reviewers should examine:                                                                                                              
                                `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` (buffer sizing, length checks)                                                                                                                    
                                `MAPIAttribute.create` and `TNEFMAPIAttribute` (data length handling)                                                                                                           
                                `TNEFAttribute.create` (attribute parsing logic)                                                                                                                                
                                `HMEFMessage` constructors and message processing loops                                                                                                                         
                                The fuzzer harness `POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` (entry point for malformed input)                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             These components together build and parse Unicode strings from the TNEF stream and appear to lack adequate bounds checks, allowing heap allocation to grow without                  
                             limit.                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Initial Issue Log                                                                                                                                                                
                             Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. **Overview and Root Cause**                                                                                                                                                      
                                The OutOfMemoryError arises because untrusted TNEF input can specify extremely large values counts and/or huge per-value lengths for variable-length fields                    
                             (ASCII_STRING, UNICODE_STRING, DIRECTORY, BINARY).  Those unchecked integers drive `IOUtils.safelyAllocate(len, MAX_RECORD_LENGTH)` to allocate massive byte                        
                             arrays, and for Unicode strings trigger a huge `char[]` in `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`, exhausting the heap.                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. **Key Preservation Points**                                                                                                                                                      
                                - We must preserve existing parsing logic in `MAPIAttribute.create`, including proper boundary alignment (`skipToBoundary`) and the dispatch to                                  
                             `MAPIStringAttribute`, `MAPIDateAttribute`, etc.                                                                                                                                    
                                - We must not alter harness code or fuzzing flagsinvalid inputs should still be rejected via IOExceptions, not by modifying fuzzer behavior.                                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. **Define Safe Limits**                                                                                                                                                           
                                - **MAX_RECORD_LENGTH** already exists for overall binary size; it remains the upper bound for any single blob.                                                                  
                                - Introduce a new constant, e.g.                                                                                                                                                 
                                    ```java                                                                                                                                                                      
                                    private static final int MAX_MAPI_VALUES = 1024;                                                                                                                             
                                    ```                                                                                                                                                                          
                                  to cap how many repeated values a multi-valued property can contain.                                                                                                           
                                - Re-use `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` to cap individual value lengths across all variable-length types.                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. **Patch Points**                                                                                                                                                                 
                                a. **After reading `values` count** (around line 188190 in MAPIAttribute.create):                                                                                               
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   int values = 1;                                                                                                                                                               
                                   if (isMV || isVL) {                                                                                                                                                           
                                       values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                       
                                       // NEW BOUNDS CHECK:                                                                                                                                                      
                                       if (values < 0 || values > MAX_MAPI_VALUES) {                                                                                                                             
                                           throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: unreasonable MAPI value count: " + values);                                                                                      
                                       }                                                                                                                                                                         
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                b. **In `getLength(type, inp)`** (around line 230232):                                                                                                                          
                                   ```java                                                                                                                                                                       
                                   int len = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                          
                                   // NEW BOUNDS CHECK:                                                                                                                                                          
                                   if (len < 0 || len > MAX_RECORD_LENGTH) {                                                                                                                                     
                                       throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: declared length " + len +                                                                                                            
                                                             " out of bounds (0" + MAX_RECORD_LENGTH + ")");                                                                                                    
                                   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                                   return len;                                                                                                                                                                   
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                c. **[Optional]** For extra defense, you can also guard fixed-length types, though they already return small constants.                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. **Error Handling**                                                                                                                                                               
                                - By throwing `IOException` early on malformed or malicious lengths/counts, we preserve the existing exception-driven rejection path, preventing any large                       
                             allocations in `IOUtils.safelyAllocate` or `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`.                                                                                                           
                                - Fuzzer harnesses catch IOExceptions and move on, eliminating OOM crashes in the target code.                                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. **Justification**                                                                                                                                                                
                                - **Optimality**: Bound checks are minimal-invasive, slot directly into existing methods, and impose no new allocations.                                                         
                                - **Preserves Logic**: Legitimate TNEF messages with small numbers of values and reasonable lengths continue parsing unchanged.  Boundary padding, type                          
                             dispatch, and string conversion logic remain intact.                                                                                                                                
                                - **Addresses Symptom & Root**: We eliminate the unbounded loop count and allocation size that directly lead to heap exhaustion.                                                 
                                - **Side Effects**: Messages with extremely large arrays or huge embedded strings will now be rejected (throw IOException).  If downstream users require larger                  
                             limits, they can tune `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` or `MAX_MAPI_VALUES` within safe operational bounds.                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             7. **Regression Safety**                                                                                                                                                            
                                - No external libraries or fuzz harnesses are modified.                                                                                                                          
                                - Existing unit tests and TNEF parsing tests should still pass; on malicious inputs, the code now raises an IOException rather than OOME.                                        
                                - You may add new unit tests that feed a crafted length/count just above the limit and assert an IOException is thrown.                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             8. **Next Steps**                                                                                                                                                                   
                                - Implement the patches in `MAPIAttribute.java`.                                                                                                                                 
                                - Run full POI test suite and re-run the Jazzer harness to confirm the OOM no longer occurs and that the fuzzer reports IOExceptions instead.                                    
                                - If desired, review other HMEF parsing entry points (`TNEFAttribute.create`, `HMEFMessage`) for similar unbounded loops or size checks, applying analogous                      
                             bounds checks where needed.                                                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                     
                             ===Evaluation End===

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             A Java fuzzing run on Apache POIs TNEF (HMEF) parser produced an OutOfMemoryError when constructing very large strings in `MAPIAttribute.create`. An attempted                     
                             patch added two sanity-check constants (`MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`, `MAX_MAPI_VALUES`) and related bounds checks around the number of values and declared length. After                    
                             applying the patch, the build fails in the `poi-scratchpad` module with syntax errors in `MAPIAttribute.java` (class, interface, or enum expected), indicating                    
                             that the new constants were placed outside any class or interface body.                                                                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - A Jazzer fuzz target in `POIHMEFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` triggered                                                                                                              
                               `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`                                                                                                                                     
                               while calling into                                                                                                                                                                
                               `org.apache.poi.hmef.attribute.MAPIAttribute.create`.                                                                                                                             
                             - The stack trace shows repeated recursion through POIs TNEF/MAPI attribute parsing, specifically when calling                                                                     
                               `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`  `new String(...)`.                                                                                                                                
                             - This suggests the parser can be made to allocate extremely large byte arrays or strings, exhausting the JVM heap.                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Attempt                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - In `poi-scratchpad/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/hmef/attribute/MAPIAttribute.java`, three new constants were introduced:                                                          
                                  `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH = IOUtils.DEFAULT_MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`                                                                                                                       
                                  `MAX_MAPI_VALUES   = 1024`                                                                                                                                                    
                                  `HEADER_SIZE       = 8`                                                                                                                                                       
                             - Two additional checks were added in the attribute creation logic:                                                                                                                 
                                 1. After reading the number of values (`values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp)`), throw an `IOException` if `values` is negative or exceeds `MAX_MAPI_VALUES`.                      
                                 2. When reading a type that has a length field, check that the declared `len` is within `[0, MAX_RECORD_LENGTH]`, otherwise throw an `IOException`.                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch Result                                                                                                                                                                        
                             - Compilation of the main modules completes with warnings, but the `poi-scratchpad` module fails on three syntax errors:                                                            
                                 error: class, interface, or enum expected                                                                                                                                       
                                   private static final int MAX_RECORD_LENGTH =                                                                                                                                 
                             - All three errors point to the newly inserted constant declarations. The build log indicates these lines appear outside any class or interface declaration,                        
                             causing the Java compiler to reject them.                                                                                                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                     
                             1. **Patch Placement in MAPIAttribute.java**                                                                                                                                        
                                - Verify the patch insert location. The new `private static final` fields must be declared inside the `public class MAPIAttribute { ... }` scope, not before the                 
                             `package` or `import` statements.                                                                                                                                                   
                                - Confirm that necessary imports (e.g., `org.apache.commons.io.IOUtils`) are present.                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. **MAPIAttribute Creation Logic**                                                                                                                                                 
                                - Examine the full method where bounds checks were inserted, ensuring that variables like `inp`, `type`, `isMV`, `isVL`, and `LittleEndian` are in scope.                        
                                - Review how multi-valued (MV) and variable-length (VL) attributes are parsed to identify all points where untrusted length fields enter object construction.                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. **Build Configuration for poi-scratchpad**                                                                                                                                       
                                - Ensure that the scratchpad submodules source directory and packaging are correctly configured so that modifications to `MAPIAttribute.java` are included and                  
                             compiled.                                                                                                                                                                           
                                - Check for any differences in Java source layout between the main `poi` module and `poi-scratchpad`.                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. **Dependency Imports**                                                                                                                                                           
                                - Confirm that `IOUtils.DEFAULT_MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` is resolvable in the scratchpad context; the patch assumes `IOUtils` is imported from Apache Commons IO.                      
                                - Cross-check that other utility classes (e.g., `LittleEndian`) are accessible without additional import or classpath adjustments.                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. **Holistic Fuzzing Safety**                                                                                                                                                      
                                - While not the root cause, review the harness in `POIHMEFFuzzer.java` to understand how inputs feed into HMEF parsing.                                                          
                                - Identify other parsing entry points for similar unbounded reads (e.g., other attribute types, different record parsers) to ensure consistent bounds                            
                             enforcement across the codebase.

                             41:public class MAPIAttribute {                                                                                                                                                     
                             42:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             43:   //arbitrarily selected; may need to increase

                             80:   public int getType() {

                             82:   }

                             86:   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                             87:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             88:   public String toString() {                                                                                                                                                    
                             89:      String hex;                                                                                                                                                                
                             90:      if(data.length <= 16) {                                                                                                                                                    
                             91:         hex = HexDump.toHex(data);                                                                                                                                              
                             92:      } else {                                                                                                                                                                   
                             93:         byte[] d = Arrays.copyOf(data, 16);                                                                                                                                     
                             94:         hex = HexDump.toHex(d);                                                                                                                                                 
                             95:         hex = hex.substring(0, hex.length()-1) + ", ....]";                                                                                                                     
                             96:      }                                                                                                                                                                          
                             97:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             98:      return property + " " + hex;                                                                                                                                               
                             99:   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                             100:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             101:   /**                                                                                                                                                                          
                             102:    * Parses a MAPI Properties TNEF Attribute, and returns                                                                                                                      
                             103:    *  the list of MAPI Attributes contained within it                                                                                                                          
                             104:    */                                                                                                                                                                          
                             105:   public static List<MAPIAttribute> create(TNEFAttribute parent) throws IOException {                                                                                          
                             106:      if(parent.getProperty() == TNEFProperty.ID_MAPIPROPERTIES) {                                                                                                              
                             107:         // Regular MAPI Properties, normally on the message                                                                                                                    
                             108:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             109:      else if(parent.getProperty() == TNEFProperty.ID_ATTACHMENT) {                                                                                                             
                             110:         // MAPI Properties for an attachment                                                                                                                                   
                             111:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             112:      else {                                                                                                                                                                    
                             113:         // Something else, oh dear...                                                                                                                                          
                             114:         throw new IllegalArgumentException(                                                                                                                                    
                             115:               "Can only create from a MAPIProperty attribute, " +                                                                                                              
                             116:               "instead received a " + parent.getProperty() + " one"                                                                                                            
                             117:         );                                                                                                                                                                     
                             118:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             119:      try(UnsynchronizedByteArrayInputStream inp = UnsynchronizedByteArrayInputStream.builder().setByteArray(parent.getData()).get()) {                                         
                             120:         // First up, get the number of attributes                                                                                                                              
                             121:         int count = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                 
                             122:         List<MAPIAttribute> attrs = new ArrayList<>();                                                                                                                         
                             123:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             124:         // Now, read each one in in turn                                                                                                                                       
                             125:         for(int i=0; i<count; i++) {                                                                                                                                           
                             126:            int typeAndMV = LittleEndian.readUShort(inp);                                                                                                                       
                             127:            int id = LittleEndian.readUShort(inp);                                                                                                                              
                             128:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             129:            // Is it either Multi-Valued or Variable-Length?                                                                                                                    
                             130:            boolean isMV = false;                                                                                                                                               
                             131:            boolean isVL = false;                                                                                                                                               
                             132:            int typeId = typeAndMV;                                                                                                                                             
                             133:            if( (typeAndMV & Types.MULTIVALUED_FLAG) != 0 ) {                                                                                                                   
                             134:               isMV = true;                                                                                                                                                     
                             135:               typeId -= Types.MULTIVALUED_FLAG;                                                                                                                                
                             136:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             137:            if(typeId == Types.ASCII_STRING.getId() || typeId == Types.UNICODE_STRING.getId() ||                                                                                
                             138:                    typeId == Types.BINARY.getId() || typeId == Types.DIRECTORY.getId()) {                                                                                      
                             139:               isVL = true;                                                                                                                                                     
                             140:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </code>                                                                                                                                                                             
                             <code>                                                                                                                                                                              
                             poi-scratchpad/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/hmef/attribute/MAPIAttribute.java:160-200                                                                                               
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             160:               if(mptype == 0) {                                                                                                                                                
                             161:                  // It's based on a normal one                                                                                                                                 
                             162:                  int mpid = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                         
                             163:                  MAPIProperty base = MAPIProperty.get(mpid);                                                                                                                   
                             164:                  name = base.name;                                                                                                                                             
                             165:               } else {                                                                                                                                                         
                             166:                  // Custom name was stored                                                                                                                                     
                             167:                  int mplen = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                        
                             168:                  if (mplen < 0) {                                                                                                                                              
                             169:                     throw new IOException("Did not expect negative value: " + mplen);                                                                                          
                             170:                  }                                                                                                                                                             
                             171:                  byte[] mpdata = new byte[mplen];                                                                                                                              
                             172:                  if (IOUtils.readFully(inp, mpdata) < 0) {                                                                                                                     
                             173:                     throw new IOException("Not enough data to read " + mplen + " bytes for attribute name");

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. **Relocate and declare constants within the class body**                                                                                                                         
                                - Remove the three constant declarations currently sitting outside the `public class MAPIAttribute {  }` scope (lines 1924).                                                   
                                - Inside the class, immediately after the existing constants at lines 4346, add:                                                                                                
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                    // maximum number of MAPI values to guard against OOM via multi-valued attributes                                                                                            
                                    private static final int MAX_MAPI_VALUES = 1024;                                                                                                                             
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - (Optional) If you wish to keep the headersize guard from the previous patch, you can likewise declare it here:                                                                
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                    private static final int HEADER_SIZE = 8;                                                                                                                                    
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                This ensures no class, interface, or enum expected errors, since all new fields now lie within the class.                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. **Enforce bounds on the number of multi-valued entries**                                                                                                                         
                                - In the `create(...)` method, locate the snippet where the code reads the value count:                                                                                          
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                      int values = 1;                                                                                                                                                            
                                      if (isMV || isVL) {                                                                                                                                                        
                                          values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                    
                                      }                                                                                                                                                                          
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Immediately after reading into `values`, insert:                                                                                                                               
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                      if (values < 0 || values > MAX_MAPI_VALUES) {                                                                                                                              
                                          throw new IOException(                                                                                                                                                 
                                              "Corrupt TNEF: unreasonable MAPI value count: " + values                                                                                                           
                                          );                                                                                                                                                                     
                                      }                                                                                                                                                                          
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                This bounds the loop iterations, preventing a crafted header from triggering huge memory allocations or DoS.                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. **Enforce bounds on declared lengths of variable-length types**                                                                                                                  
                                - In the `getLength(int type, InputStream inp)` helper, locate the branch for types that carry a length:                                                                         
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                    // before patch:                                                                                                                                                             
                                    if (type == Types.ASCII_STRING.getId() ||                                                                                                                                    
                                        type == Types.UNICODE_STRING.getId() ||                                                                                                                                  
                                        type == Types.BINARY.getId() ||                                                                                                                                          
                                        type == Types.DIRECTORY.getId()) {                                                                                                                                       
                                        return LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                        
                                    }                                                                                                                                                                            
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Replace this with:                                                                                                                                                             
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                    if (type == Types.ASCII_STRING.getId()                                                                                                                                       
                                        || type == Types.UNICODE_STRING.getId()                                                                                                                                  
                                        || type == Types.BINARY.getId()                                                                                                                                          
                                        || type == Types.DIRECTORY.getId()) {                                                                                                                                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                        int len = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                     
                                        // sanity check on declared length                                                                                                                                       
                                        if (len < 0 || len > getMaxRecordLength()) {                                                                                                                             
                                            throw new IOException(                                                                                                                                               
                                                "Corrupt TNEF: declared length " + len +                                                                                                                         
                                                " out of bounds (0" + getMaxRecordLength() + ")"                                                                                                                
                                            );                                                                                                                                                                   
                                        }                                                                                                                                                                        
                                        return len;                                                                                                                                                              
                                    }                                                                                                                                                                            
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - This uses the existing `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` (editable via `setMaxRecordLength`) to guard every length field, avoiding excessively large buffer reads.                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. **Leverage IOUtils.safelyAllocate for final allocation**                                                                                                                         
                                - The allocation site already does:                                                                                                                                              
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                    byte[] data = IOUtils.safelyAllocate(len, MAX_RECORD_LENGTH);                                                                                                                
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - By pairing the precheck in `getLength` with `safelyAllocate`, we have two layers of defense: a fast failure on unreasonable declared lengths and a guaranteed                 
                             cap in the allocator.                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. **Validate imports and build**                                                                                                                                                   
                                - Confirm `import org.apache.poi.util.IOUtils;` remains in the file (it already is present).                                                                                     
                                - No new external dependencies are required.                                                                                                                                     
                                - Rebuild `poi-scratchpad`; the syntax errors will be resolved since all fields are inside the class scope.                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             **Justification**                                                                                                                                                                   
                             - Moving the constants inside the class restores valid Java syntax and preserves existing logic.                                                                                    
                             - Bounding both the number of values (`MAX_MAPI_VALUES`) and the declared length (`MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`) neutralizes fuzzing inputs that previously led to                            
                             `OutOfMemoryError`.                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - We continue to support the same fuzzing harness unchanged; only the core parser is hardened.                                                                                      
                             - This two-tier check pattern (validate header, then safely allocate) mirrors similar bounds enforcement elsewhere in POI, ensuring consistency.                                    
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Potential side effects are minimal: legitimate but extremely large MAPI attributes beyond 1 000 000 bytes or 1024 entries will now throw an `IOException` early.                    
                             Callers of `MAPIAttribute.create` already expect `IOException` on corrupt or unsupported input, so existing error-handling paths remain valid.                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>
