                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             The initial issue is a Java `OutOfMemoryError` triggered during fuzzing of Apache POIs HMEF (TNEF) support. The stack trace shows a large string allocation in                     
                             `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE`, called from `MAPIAttribute.create`. An attempted patch introduced two new limits in                                                                  
                             `poi-scratchpad/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/hmef/attribute/MAPIAttribute.java`:                                                                                                    
                             - A maximum record length (`MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`) check for all variable-length fields.                                                                                               
                             - A maximum MAPI value count (`MAX_MAPI_VALUES`) check for multi-valued attributes.                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Despite these additions, the same OOM crash remains, indicating that some unbounded path still allows overly large memory allocations.                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - Exception:                                                                                                                                                                     
                                  com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory                                                                                                         
                                  Caused by: java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space                                                                                                                         
                                - Stack trace highlights:                                                                                                                                                        
                                   `String.<init>(String.java:657)`                                                                                                                                             
                                   `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE(StringUtil.java:94)`                                                                                                                            
                                   `MAPIAttribute.create(MAPIAttribute.java:175)`                                                                                                                               
                                   `TNEFMAPIAttribute.<init>(TNEFMAPIAttribute.java:41)`                                                                                                                        
                                   `HMEFMessage.processMessage(HMEFMessage.java:105)`                                                                                                                           
                                - Observation: the code reads a length or count from the input without sufficient upper bounds, and then constructs a Java `String` from the raw bytes, allowing                 
                             an attacker-supplied large length to consume the heap.                                                                                                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Patch Attempt                                                                                                                                                                    
                                Modifications in `MAPIAttribute.java` around the methods that read lengths and counts:                                                                                           
                                - Added constants:                                                                                                                                                               
                                   `DEFAULT_MAX_RECORD_LENGTH = 1_000_000`                                                                                                                                      
                                   `MAX_MAPI_VALUES = 1024`                                                                                                                                                     
                                   `HEADER_SIZE = 8`                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Changed the logic for multi-valued (MV/VL) attributes:                                                                                                                         
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                            
                                  if (values < 0 || values > MAX_MAPI_VALUES) {                                                                                                                                  
                                      throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: unreasonable MAPI value count: " + values);                                                                                           
                                  }                                                                                                                                                                              
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Changed the logic for variable-length fields:                                                                                                                                  
                                  ```java                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  int len = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                           
                                  if (len < 0 || len > MAX_RECORD_LENGTH) {                                                                                                                                      
                                      throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: declared length " + len +                                                                                                             
                                                            " out of bounds (0" + MAX_RECORD_LENGTH + ")");                                                                                                     
                                  }                                                                                                                                                                              
                                  return len;                                                                                                                                                                    
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                These checks are intended to abort parsing when an attacker claims a very large length or count.                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Result After Patch                                                                                                                                                               
                                - The fuzzer still reproduces the same OOM at `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` (now line 177 in the patched file).                                                                  
                                - The exception and stack trace remain the same, indicating that the new bounds checks did not cover the path leading to the huge string allocation.                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                  
                                To understand why the OOM persists, the following parts of the codebase should be reviewed:                                                                                      
                                - All branches in `MAPIAttribute.create` where byte lengths are read (including fixed- and variable-length string handling), ensuring each length is checked                     
                             before allocation.                                                                                                                                                                  
                                - The interaction between `TNEFAttribute.create`, `TNEFMAPIAttribute`, and `HMEFMessage.processMessage` to see if lengths are still coming from headers or                       
                             sub-attributes that bypass the new checks.                                                                                                                                          
                                - The implementation of `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE` to confirm how many bytes it consumes and whether the length parameter it receives is always vetted                        
                             upstream.                                                                                                                                                                           
                                - Any code paths that build combined or nested data structures (e.g., multi-valued strings) where intermediate lengths or counts might not be limited by                         
                             `MAX_MAPI_VALUES` or `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`.

                             92:        }                                                                                                                                                                        
                             93:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             94:        return new String(string, offset, len * 2, UTF16LE);                                                                                                                     
                             95:    }

                             101:     * <p>

                             105:     * @return the converted string, never {@code null}                                                                                                                         
                             106:     */                                                                                                                                                                         
                             107:    public static String getFromUnicodeLE(byte[] string) {                                                                                                                      
                             108:        if (string.length == 0) {                                                                                                                                               
                             109:            return "";                                                                                                                                                          
                             110:        }                                                                                                                                                                       
                             111:        return getFromUnicodeLE(string, 0, string.length / 2);                                                                                                                  
                             112:    }

                             140:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             141:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             142:            // Turn the type ID into a strongly typed thing                                                                                                                     
                             143:            MAPIType type = Types.getById(typeId);                                                                                                                              
                             144:            if (type == null) {                                                                                                                                                 
                             145:               type = Types.createCustom(typeId);                                                                                                                               
                             146:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             147:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             148:            // If it's a named property, rather than a standard                                                                                                                 
                             149:            //  MAPI property, grab the details of it                                                                                                                           
                             150:            MAPIProperty prop = MAPIProperty.get(id);                                                                                                                           
                             151:            if(id >= 0x8000 && id <= 0xFFFF) {                                                                                                                                  
                             152:               byte[] guid = new byte[16];                                                                                                                                      
                             153:               if (IOUtils.readFully(inp, guid) < 0) {                                                                                                                          
                             154:                  throw new IOException("Not enough data to read guid");                                                                                                        
                             155:               }                                                                                                                                                                
                             156:               int mptype = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                          
                             157:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             158:               // Get the name of it                                                                                                                                            
                             159:               String name;                                                                                                                                                     
                             160:               if(mptype == 0) {                                                                                                                                                
                             161:                  // It's based on a normal one                                                                                                                                 
                             162:                  int mpid = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                         
                             163:                  MAPIProperty base = MAPIProperty.get(mpid);                                                                                                                   
                             164:                  name = base.name;                                                                                                                                             
                             165:               } else {                                                                                                                                                         
                             166:                  // Custom name was stored                                                                                                                                     
                             167:                  int mplen = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                        
                             168:                  if (mplen < 0) {                                                                                                                                              
                             169:                     throw new IOException("Did not expect negative value: " + mplen);                                                                                          
                             170:                  }                                                                                                                                                             
                             171:                  byte[] mpdata = new byte[mplen];                                                                                                                              
                             172:                  if (IOUtils.readFully(inp, mpdata) < 0) {                                                                                                                     
                             173:                     throw new IOException("Not enough data to read " + mplen + " bytes for attribute name");                                                                   
                             174:                  }                                                                                                                                                             
                             175:                  name = StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE(mpdata, 0, (mplen/2)-1);                                                                                                   
                             176:                  skipToBoundary(mplen, inp);                                                                                                                                   
                             177:               }                                                                                                                                                                
                             178:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             179:               // Now create                                                                                                                                                    
                             180:               prop = MAPIProperty.createCustom(id, type, name);                                                                                                                
                             181:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             182:            if(prop == MAPIProperty.UNKNOWN) {                                                                                                                                  
                             183:               prop = MAPIProperty.createCustom(id, type, "(unknown " + Integer.toHexString(id) + ")");                                                                         
                             184:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             185:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             186:            // Now read in the value(s)                                                                                                                                         
                             187:            int values = 1;                                                                                                                                                     
                             188:            if(isMV || isVL) {                                                                                                                                                  
                             189:               values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                              
                             190:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             191:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             192:            if (type == Types.NULL && values > 1) {                                                                                                                             
                             193:               throw new IOException("Placeholder/NULL arrays aren't supported.");                                                                                              
                             194:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             195:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             196:            for(int j=0; j<values; j++) {                                                                                                                                       
                             197:               int len = getLength(type, inp);                                                                                                                                  
                             198:               byte[] data = IOUtils.safelyAllocate(len, MAX_RECORD_LENGTH);                                                                                                    
                             199:               inp.read(data);                                                                                                                                                  
                             200:               skipToBoundary(len, inp);                                                                                                                                        
                             201:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             202:               // Create                                                                                                                                                        
                             203:               MAPIAttribute attr;                                                                                                                                              
                             204:               if(type == Types.UNICODE_STRING || type == Types.ASCII_STRING) {                                                                                                 
                             205:                  attr = new MAPIStringAttribute(prop, typeId, data);                                                                                                           
                             206:               } else if(type == Types.APP_TIME || type == Types.TIME) {                                                                                                        
                             207:                  attr = new MAPIDateAttribute(prop, typeId, data);                                                                                                             
                             208:               } else if(id == MAPIProperty.RTF_COMPRESSED.id) {                                                                                                                
                             209:                  attr = new MAPIRtfAttribute(prop, typeId, data);                                                                                                              
                             210:               } else {                                                                                                                                                         
                             211:                  attr = new MAPIAttribute(prop, typeId, data);                                                                                                                 
                             212:               }                                                                                                                                                                
                             213:               attrs.add(attr);                                                                                                                                                 
                             214:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             215:         }                                                                                                                                                                      
                             216:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             217:         // All done                                                                                                                                                            
                             218:         return attrs;                                                                                                                                                          
                             219:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             220:   }                                                                                                                                                                            
                             221:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             222:   private static int getLength(MAPIType type, InputStream inp) throws IOException {                                                                                            
                             223:      if (type.isFixedLength()) {                                                                                                                                               
                             224:         return type.getLength();                                                                                                                                               
                             225:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             226:      if (type == Types.ASCII_STRING ||                                                                                                                                         
                             227:          type == Types.UNICODE_STRING ||                                                                                                                                       
                             228:          type == Types.DIRECTORY ||                                                                                                                                            
                             229:          type == Types.BINARY) {                                                                                                                                               
                             230:            // Need to read the length, as it varies                                                                                                                            
                             231:            return LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                   
                             232:      } else {                                                                                                                                                                  
                             233:            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown type " + type);                                                                                                         
                             234:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             235:   }                                                                                                                                                                            
                             236:   private static void skipToBoundary(int length, InputStream inp) throws IOException {                                                                                         
                             237:      // Data is always padded out to a 4 byte boundary                                                                                                                         
                             238:      if(length % 4 != 0) {                                                                                                                                                     
                             239:         int toSkip = 4 - (length % 4);                                                                                                                                         
                             240:         inp.skip(toSkip);                                                                                                                                                      
                             241:      }                                                                                                                                                                         
                             242:   }                                                                                                                                                                            
                             243:}

                             27:/**

                             32:   private final List<MAPIAttribute> attributes;                                                                                                                                 
                             33:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             34:   /**                                                                                                                                                                           
                             35:    * Constructs a single new mapi containing attribute from the                                                                                                                 
                             36:    *  id, type, and the contents of the stream                                                                                                                                  
                             37:    */                                                                                                                                                                           
                             38:   protected TNEFMAPIAttribute(int id, int type, InputStream inp) throws IOException {                                                                                           
                             39:      super(id, type, inp);                                                                                                                                                      
                             40:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             41:      attributes = MAPIAttribute.create(this);                                                                                                                                   
                             42:   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                             43:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             44:   public List<MAPIAttribute> getMAPIAttributes() {                                                                                                                              
                             45:      return attributes;                                                                                                                                                         
                             46:   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                             47:                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             48:   public String toString() {                                                                                                                                                    
                             49:      return "Attribute " + getProperty() + ", type=" + getType() +                                                                                                              
                             50:             ", " + attributes.size() + " MAPI Attributes";                                                                                                                      
                             51:   }                                                                                                                                                                             
                             52:}

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Reapply and centralize previous limit constants                                                                                                                                  
                                - Ensure `DEFAULT_MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`, `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH`, `MAX_RECORD_COUNT`, `MAX_MAPI_VALUES`, and `HEADER_SIZE` are defined once at the top of                               
                             MAPIAttribute.java (as already introduced), to govern all bounds checks.                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Bound the initial attribute count                                                                                                                                                
                                - In `MAPIAttribute.create(...)`, right after reading                                                                                                                            
                                     int count = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                      
                                  insert:                                                                                                                                                                        
                                     if (count < 0 || count > MAX_RECORD_COUNT) {                                                                                                                                
                                         throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: unreasonable MAPI attribute count: " + count);                                                                                     
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                  This prevents a massive loop driving OOM.                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Harden the custom-name path                                                                                                                                                      
                                - Replace the unchecked                                                                                                                                                          
                                     byte[] mpdata = new byte[mplen];                                                                                                                                            
                                  with a safely-bounded allocation:                                                                                                                                              
                                     if (mplen < 0 || mplen > MAX_RECORD_LENGTH) {                                                                                                                               
                                         throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: attribute name length " + mplen +                                                                                                  
                                                               " out of bounds (0" + MAX_RECORD_LENGTH + ")");                                                                                                  
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     byte[] mpdata = IOUtils.safelyAllocate(mplen, MAX_RECORD_LENGTH);                                                                                                           
                                - This guards against pathological `mplen` values and reuses IOUtilss proven checks.                                                                                            
                                - The subsequent call to `StringUtil.getFromUnicodeLE(mpdata, 0, (mplen/2)-1)` is now safe, since `mplen`  MAX_RECORD_LENGTH  `(mplen/2)-1`                                   
                             ~MAX_RECORD_LENGTH/2.                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Enforce per-attribute value count limits                                                                                                                                         
                                - Reapply (and consolidate) the MV/VL `values` bounds check so that every multi-value branch does:                                                                               
                                     int values = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                     
                                     if (values < 0 || values > MAX_MAPI_VALUES) {                                                                                                                               
                                         throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: unreasonable MAPI value count: " + values);                                                                                        
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                - This is already partially in the last patch, but confirm it appears in both attribute-level loops and covers all `isMV`/`isVL` cases.                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Bound all variable-length fields in getLength                                                                                                                                    
                                - In `private static int getLength(...)`, after                                                                                                                                  
                                     int len = LittleEndian.readInt(inp);                                                                                                                                        
                                  add:                                                                                                                                                                           
                                     if (len < 0 || len > MAX_RECORD_LENGTH) {                                                                                                                                   
                                         throw new IOException("Corrupt TNEF: declared length " + len +                                                                                                          
                                                               " out of bounds (0" + MAX_RECORD_LENGTH + ")");                                                                                                  
                                     }                                                                                                                                                                           
                                - This ensures no downstream code (including `IOUtils.safelyAllocate` or `skipToBoundary`) ever sees a maliciously large length.                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Integration and testing                                                                                                                                                          
                                - Maintain existing exception types (`IOException`) so that corrupt-input semantics remain unchanged.                                                                            
                                - Run the HMEF fuzzer and full test suite to confirm:                                                                                                                            
                                   The OOM is eliminated under large-length fuzz inputs.                                                                                                                        
                                   No regressions occur when parsing valid documents close to, but within, the new limits.                                                                                      
                                - If legitimate inputs hit the new caps, consider adjusting `MAX_RECORD_LENGTH` or `MAX_MAPI_VALUES` upwards in a controlled fashion.                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Justification:                                                                                                                                                                      
                             - The persistent OOM stemmed from unchecked `count`, `mplen`, and `len` values. By systematically bounding each untrusted integer before any allocation or loop, we                 
                             eliminate all attack surfaces that produce huge arrays or loops.                                                                                                                    
                             - External library calls (e.g., `StringUtil`) remain unmodified; we preserve their semantics strictly by vetting inputs upstream.                                                   
                             - Existing multi-valued attribute logic (`values` loops) is preserved, only capped to a safe maximum.                                                                               
                             - Using `IOUtils.safelyAllocate` for variable-sized buffers unifies allocation checks and ensures consistency across the codebase.                                                  
                             - The approach avoids broad exception catches, and does not touch harness, fuzzing, or test code, so existing tests and fuzz harness remain valid.                                  
                             - Similar patterns exist in other parts of POI (e.g., bounding record lengths in POIFS and HSSF), ensuring consistency with project-wide safety practices.
